We actively block them by default, helping you evade hackers, scammers, and data-hungry companies.</p>

               <h2 class="single-column-feature-card_headingText___e8GC heading_heading2__WFJ4M heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">Block most ads & cookie pop-ups for fewer interruptions.</h2>

              </div>

              <p class="text text_text-md__BCPnT text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi single-column-feature-card_mainText__fZhD4">Our tracker blocking stops most ads before they even appear, letting you enjoy your favorite content with less hassle. We spot cookie pop-ups right away and, where possible, opt you out automatically, so you won’t even see them.</p>

               <h2 class="single-column-feature-card_headingText___e8GC heading_heading2__WFJ4M heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">Data protection, not data collection.</h2>

              </div>

              <p class="text text_text-md__BCPnT text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi single-column-feature-card_mainText__fZhD4">We believe the best way to protect your data is to stop it from being collected at all. We never track your searches, and our browsing protections help stop other companies from collecting your data.</p>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="2" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--1" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--1"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">How does DuckDuckGo protect my privacy?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--1" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--1">

                   <div class="stack_root__raz5U" style="--gap-size: 1.5rem;">

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">If you’re like most people on the Internet, you use Google to search the web and Google Chrome to browse the web. That means, by default, Google can keep track of every single search you make and website you visit. On those websites, other companies may also track you.</p>

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">DuckDuckGo is an independent Google alternative that also lets you search and browse the web, but we don’t track your searches or browsing history, and our <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/get-duckduckgo/does-duckduckgo-make-a-browser/">browsers</a> and <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/desktop/adding-duckduckgo-to-your-browser/">extensions</a> help you block other companies from trying to track you as well, all by default. Our free browser comes with seamless protection built-in, including <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/">tracker blocking</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/#smarter-encryption-https-upgrading">increased encryption</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/email-protection/what-is-duckduckgo-email-protection/">email protection</a>, and more, making it the most comprehensive protection you can get with one download. Plus, <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy-pro/">DuckDuckGo subscribers</a> get four additional features: a fast and simple <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy-pro/vpn/">VPN</a>, access to advanced AI models in <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/duckai">Duck.ai</a>, a <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy-pro/personal-information-removal/">Personal Information Removal</a> service, and an <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy-pro/identity-theft-restoration/">Identity Theft Restoration</a> service. That’s how DuckDuckGo helps protect you in a nutshell. <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/company/how-does-duckduckgo-protect-privacy/">Learn more</a></p>

                   </div>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="3" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--2" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--2"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">Does DuckDuckGo block all trackers on websites I visit?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--2" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--2">

                   <div class="stack_root__raz5U" style="--gap-size: 1.5rem;">

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">DuckDuckGo <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/privacy">never tracks you</a>. And when you leave our search engine and use our browsers or extensions to visit other sites, we aim to protect your privacy as much as possible. No service can eliminate all hidden tracking or all profiling online because trackers are always trying to evade specific protections. To be effective, our protections continually evolve to mitigate this while avoiding website breakage. That’s also why we offer multiple types of <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/">web tracking protections</a>.</p>

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">Other browsers offer some of these by default, like cookie and fingerprinting protections, but we also provide many other protections that most browsers do not offer by default, like <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/#3rd-party-tracker-loading-protection">3rd-Party Tracker Loading Protection</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/#global-privacy-control-gpc">Global Privacy Control</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/#link-tracking-protection">Link Tracking Protection</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/#cname-cloaking-protection">CNAME Cloaking Protection</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/#google-amp-protection">Google AMP Protection</a>, and <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/">more</a>, which all help cover different tracking angles. Our <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://github.com/duckduckgo/tracker-blocklists">list of trackers</a> is open source, along with the <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://github.com/duckduckgo/privacy-configuration">list of exceptions</a> we make to preserve usability. <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections">Learn more</a></p>

                   </div>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="4" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--3" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--3"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">How many people use DuckDuckGo?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--3" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--3">

                   <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">Our best guess — over 100 million people! We don’t track our users, so it’s impossible for us to know how many people in total actually use our product. However, we can make an estimate based on the number of searches we get each month. Thanks to all these users, DuckDuckGo <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/cloudflare-radar-report">holds the #2 position in mobile search market share</a> in the US, and 20 other markets including the United Kingdom, Canada, Australia, Poland, Italy, and Spain.</p>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="5" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--4" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--4"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">How does DuckDuckGo make money?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--4" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--4">

                   <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">We make money from private ads on our search engine. On other search engines, ads are based on profiles compiled from your personal information, such as search, browsing, and purchase history. We don’t have that information (per our <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/privacy">Privacy Policy</a>) because search ads on DuckDuckGo are based on the search results page you’re viewing instead of on what other companies’ tracking algorithms assume about you. For example, if you search for cars, we’ll show you ads about cars. We also make money from the paid <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy-pro/">DuckDuckGo subscription</a>, our four-in-one subscription service. <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/company/how-duckduckgo-makes-money/">Learn more</a></p>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="6" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--5" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--5"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">Why use DuckDuckGo instead of Google?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--5" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--5">

                   <div class="stack_root__raz5U" style="--gap-size: 1.5rem;">

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi"><b>Use DuckDuckGo to help protect yourself online.</b> Ever get ads so creepy it feels like your phone is listening to you? Or see ads for something you searched for once following you around everywhere? If you’re wondering who to blame, it’s probably Google. For decades, they’ve been tracking your searches, embedding trackers in their Chrome browser, and hiding even more trackers on the most-popular websites. This type of mass collection of your personal information can make you vulnerable to hackers, scammers, and other privacy-invasive companies.</p>

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">DuckDuckGo lets you search and browse like you’re used to, but (unlike Google) we never track you and our browser helps block trackers from companies that run online tracking networks like Google, TikTok, and Meta (Facebook). Oh, and our browser is free — we make money from <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/company/how-duckduckgo-makes-money/">privacy-respecting search ads</a>, not by exploiting your data.</p>

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi"><b>Use DuckDuckGo to get a better online experience.</b> Have you noticed Google search results getting worse? <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://www.theatlantic.com/ideas/archive/2022/06/google-search-algorithm-internet/661325/">You’re not alone</a>. For many Google searches, most of the results on the first page are either ads or Google pushing their own services. It can be even worse on mobile.</p>

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">On DuckDuckGo, we keep ads to a minimum and our search ads are private, only based on the search results page you’re viewing, and not on you as a person. The tracker blocking that’s built in to our browser also blocks a large number of tracker-dependent ads from loading by default. Coupled with other browser features like <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/#cookie-pop-up-management">automatically blocking cookie pop-ups</a>, our default <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/privacy/web-tracking-protections/">web tracking protections</a> give you a cleaner online experience overall with DuckDuckGo.</p>

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi"><b>Use DuckDuckGo to send a message to Big Tech companies like Google who are taking away user choice online and profiting by stealing your personal information.</b> Google is the epitome of Big Tech, with their tentacles in everything, compiling detailed profiles about everyone, and making billions of dollars auctioning off access to your attention, and for what? Creepy ads that follow you around? By comparison, DuckDuckGo is a small, independent company, based in Paoli, Pennsylvania, with a vision to offer a choice to be more protected online without sacrifice to anyone who wants it.</p>

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">Use DuckDuckGo because it’s fast and secure, because it’s a free Google alternative that lets you search and browse the way you want, and because it puts you back in control of your personal data.</p>

                   </div>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="7" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--6" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--6"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">Is Incognito Mode private?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--6" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--6">

                   <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">No. It is a myth that you can't be tracked while using so-called “Incognito” mode. In fact, all Incognito mode really does is delete information on your computer. Incognito mode does nothing to stop Google from saving your searches, nor does it stop companies, Internet service providers, or governments from being able to track you online. By contrast, DuckDuckGo Search never keeps your or anyone else's search history and the DuckDuckGo browser helps keep you protected on websites too. <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/company/how-does-duckduckgo-protect-privacy/">Learn more</a></p>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="8" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--7" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--7"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">How do DuckDuckGo Search results compare to Google's?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--7" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--7">

                   <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">DuckDuckGo Search gives you truly private search results without tradeoffs in result quality. We have everything you’ve come to expect in an online search experience (images, maps, answers, etc.), and because there’s no search history on DuckDuckGo, you escape the filter bubble of manipulated results. You’ll also find <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/bangs">bonus features</a> that make our private search engine more convenient and a little more fun. We’re <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/updates">always improving</a>, so you can expect even more search improvements in the coming year! <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://spreadprivacy.com/is-duckduckgo-a-good-search-engine/">Learn more</a></p>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                 <section class="accordion_accordionItem__cB73r" value="9" data-reach-accordion-item="" data-state="collapsed">

                  <h3 class="accordion_accordionHeader__eQ9AT"><button aria-controls="panel--«rj»--8" aria-expanded="false" class="accordion_accordionTrigger__ehjD_" data-reach-accordion-button="" data-state="collapsed" id="button--«rj»--8"><span class="homeFAQ_faqHeading__dSPCw heading_heading5__s5t07 heading_heading__yebkp heading_responsive__lDUe2">Is DuckDuckGo owned by Google or any other entity?</span>

                    <svg fill="none" viewbox="0 0 16 16" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="accordion_accordionTriggerIcon__7IFG3" aria-hidden="true">

                     <path fill="currentColor" d="M11.915 5.202a.625.625 0 01.92.846L9.563 9.601c-.829.9-2.24.913-3.086.042l-.04-.042-3.272-3.553-.02-.024a.625.625 0 01.917-.846l.023.024 3.271 3.552.034.034c.35.342.918.33 1.254-.034l3.271-3.552z"></path>

                    </svg></button></h3>

                  <div hidden role="region" aria-labelledby="button--«rj»--8" class="accordion_accordionContent__k7eWV" data-reach-accordion-panel="" data-state="collapsed" id="panel--«rj»--8">

                   <div class="stack_root__raz5U" style="--gap-size: 1.5rem;">

                    <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">No, we are not and have never been owned by Google or any other entity. We have been an independent company since our founding in 2008. You may notice content originally from Google, such as YouTube videos, in our search results. Even though Google has a monopoly on access to this content, we are able to get it anonymously via indirect sources. This ensures we still offer quality search results without needing to rely on Google directly for any of it. We also offer an extension for Google Chrome and a Google Android app, but these are not in partnership with Google — and actually aim to protect you from Google’s online trackers. <a target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/company/how-does-duckduckgo-protect-privacy/">Learn more</a></p>

                   </div>

                  </div>

                 </section>

                  <h2 class="text text_text-eyebrow__GDH_m text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi footer_aboutHeading__5n2tt footer_footerHeading__iYgZ8">About DuckDuckGo</h2>

                  <div class="stack_root__raz5U" style="--gap-size: 2rem;">

                   <p class="text text_text-sm__fJ7Aa text_text__XCDHr text_text-weight-normal__Zsm0J text_responsive__YZEGi">At DuckDuckGo, we believe the best way to protect your personal information from hackers, scammers, and privacy-invasive companies is to stop it from being collected at all. That's why millions of people <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="footer_footerLink__6R85j" href="https://duckduckgo.com/compare-privacy">choose DuckDuckGo over Chrome and other browsers</a> to search and browse online. Our built-in search engine is like Google but never tracks your searches. And our browsing protections, such as ad tracker blocking and cookie blocking, help stop other companies from collecting your data. Oh, and our browser is free — we make money from <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="footer_footerLink__6R85j" href="https://duckduckgo.com/duckduckgo-help-pages/company/how-duckduckgo-makes-money">privacy-respecting search ads</a>, not by exploiting your data. Take back control of your personal information with the browser designed for data protection, not data collection. Available to download on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="footer_footerLink__6R85j" href="https://duckduckgo.com/mac?origin=funnel_home_website__details">Mac</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="footer_footerLink__6R85j" href="https://duckduckgo.com/windows?origin=funnel_home_website__details">Windows</a>, <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="footer_footerLink__6R85j" href="https://apps.apple.com/app/duckduckgo-privacy-browser/id663592361?platform=iphone">iOS</a>, and <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="footer_footerLink__6R85j" href="https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=com.duckduckgo.mobile.android&referrer=origin%3Dfunnel_home_website__details">Android</a>.</p>

                  </div>

                 </div>

                </div>
